#METABOLOMICS WORKBENCH STUDY_ID:ST000081 ANALYSIS_ID:AN000131
VERSION             	1
CREATED_ON          	2016-09-17
#PROJECT
PR:PROJECT_TITLE                 	Metabolic Profiling of Visceral and Subcutaneous Adipose Tissue from Colorectal
PR:PROJECT_TITLE                 	Patients: Unraveling the Link Between Adipose Tissue and Cancer
PR:PROJECT_TYPE                  	biomarker study
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	This West Coast Metabolomics Center pilot and feasibility project was granted
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	Johanna Lampe (Fred Hutchinson Cancer Research Center at Univ. of Washington,
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	In the current investigation, unbiased profiling of the metabolome and lipidome
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	adipose tissue samples (visceral(VAT) and subcutaenous (SAT)) and serum of 50
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	patients, including stages I-IV, from the Fred Hutchinson Cancer Center
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	and the German Cancer Research Center (Heidelberg, Germany) was conducted. The
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	and metabolome of adipose tissue (VAT/SAT) and serum were analyzed using
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	UPLC-QTOFMS analysis and GC-TOFMS analyses, respectively. The primary
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	of this project were to 1) compare the metabolome and lipidome of matched VAT
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	SAT adipose tissue of n=50 Colorectal Cancer Cell (CRC) patients, 2)
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	the associations between the lipidome and metabolome in adipose tissue
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	and serum of n=50 CRC patients and 3) test the associations between the
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	of VAT and serum with the tumor stage of CRC patients.
PR:INSTITUTE                     	University of California, Davis
PR:DEPARTMENT                    	Genome and Biomedical Sciences Facility
PR:LABORATORY                    	WCMC Metabolomics Core
PR:LAST_NAME                     	Fiehn
PR:FIRST_NAME                    	Oliver
PR:ADDRESS                       	1315 Genome and Biomedical Sciences Facility,451 Health Sciences Drive, Davis,
PR:ADDRESS                       	95616
PR:EMAIL                         	ofiehn@ucdavis.edu
PR:PHONE                         	(530) 754-8258
PR:FUNDING_SOURCE                	NIH U24DK097154
#STUDY
ST:STUDY_TITLE                   	Metabolic Profiling of Visceral and Subcutaneous Adipose Tissue from Colorectal
ST:STUDY_TITLE                   	Patients: UHPLC-QTOF MS analyis of subcutaneous and visceral adipose tissue
ST:STUDY_TYPE                    	biomarker study
ST:STUDY_SUMMARY                 	This West Coast Metabolomics Center pilot and feasibility project was granted
ST:STUDY_SUMMARY                 	Johanna Lampe (Fred Hutchinson Cancer Research Center at Univ. of Washington,
ST:STUDY_SUMMARY                 	In the current investigation, unbiased profiling of the metabolome and lipidome
ST:STUDY_SUMMARY                 	adipose tissue samples (visceral(VAT) and subcutaenous (SAT)) and serum of 50
ST:STUDY_SUMMARY                 	patients, including stages I-IV, from the Fred Hutchinson Cancer Center
ST:STUDY_SUMMARY                 	and the German Cancer Research Center (Heidelberg, Germany) was conducted. The
ST:STUDY_SUMMARY                 	and metabolome of adipose tissue (VAT/SAT) and serum were analyzed using
ST:STUDY_SUMMARY                 	UPLC-QTOFMS analysis and GC-TOFMS analyses, respectively.  The primary
ST:STUDY_SUMMARY                 	of this project were to 1) compare the metabolome and lipidome
ST:STUDY_SUMMARY                 	SAT adipose tissue of n=50 Colorectal Cancer Cell (CRC) patients, 2)
ST:STUDY_SUMMARY                 	the associations between the lipidome and metabolome in adipose tissue
ST:STUDY_SUMMARY                 	and serum of n=50 CRC patients and 3) test the associations between the
ST:STUDY_SUMMARY                 	of VAT and serum with the tumor stage of CRC patients. 
ST:INSTITUTE                     	University of California, Davis
ST:DEPARTMENT                    	Genome and Biomedical Sciences Facility
ST:LABORATORY                    	WCMC Metabolomics Core
ST:LAST_NAME                     	Fiehn
ST:FIRST_NAME                    	Oliver
ST:ADDRESS                       	1315 Genome and Biomedical Sciences Facility451 Health Sciences DriveDavis, CA
ST:EMAIL                         	ofiehn@ucdavis.edu
ST:PHONE                         	(530) 754-8258
ST:NUM_GROUPS                    	2
ST:TOTAL_SUBJECTS                	59
ST:STUDY_COMMENTS                	Lipidomics profiles for studyThis is the SAT and VAT part of the studyLabel-ID
ST:STUDY_COMMENTS                	conserved for all parts of the study---The samples had to be diluted for
ST:STUDY_COMMENTS                	mode measurements (therefore 2 dilutions are measured for the same sample).
ST:STUDY_COMMENTS                	are then combined and scaling factor is used for final results.
